### [215] [Not All Tokens Learn Alike: Attention Entropy Reveals Heterogeneous Signals in RL Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07660)
*Gengyang Li,Zheng-Fan Wu,Siqi Bao,Yunfang Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型强化学习微调过程中，不同响应token的学习信号差异性，提出用注意力熵刻画token级别异质性，并通过实验证明利用熵结构化采样和软重加权机制能显著提升模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前强化学习后训练（RL-based post-training）被广泛用来提升大语言模型的推理能力，但RL在token层面的学习信号和优化结构尚未被充分理解和挖掘。作者希望分析并利用token信号的异质性以提升训练效率和模型效果。

Method: 主要方法是用注意力熵来度量每个token上下文支持的集中/分散程度，将token分为低熵的anchor和高熵的explorer。通过实验证明这些token梯度结构不同，并提出基于熵动态的软权重重加权方法进行优化。

Result: 实验证明，token级别学习信号存在冗余，结构化采样（按注意力熵选token）下模型更新特性有显著差异。提出的动态熵感知软重加权训练，让Qwen3-8B-Base模型的held-out平均得分由34.39提升到37.40，达到了较强提升。

Conclusion: 注意力熵揭示了token级别强化学习信号的优化相关结构，说明统一平均token信号会掩盖推理微调中的重要异质性。动态结构化优化可以带来更好的模型推理提升。

Abstract: Reinforcement-learning-based post-training has become a key approach for improving the reasoning ability of large language models, but its token-level learning signals remain poorly understood. This work studies their heterogeneity through attention entropy, which measures how concentrated or diffuse the contextual support is for each response token.
  We first show that token-level RL objectives are sparsely estimable: uniformly random 20 percent token subsets preserve much of the full-token held-out performance, suggesting substantial redundancy in token-level updates. However, entropy-structured subsets behave very differently. Low-attention-entropy tokens, which we call anchors, rely on concentrated support, produce stable gradients aligned with full-token updates, and provide a reliable optimization backbone, but tend to plateau on harder benchmarks. High-attention-entropy tokens, which we call explorers, aggregate more diffuse context and induce larger but more volatile gradients. Explorer-only training is unstable on average, though rare successful runs suggest that these tokens may contain useful hard-reasoning signals when optimization remains stable.
  We support this anchor-explorer spectrum with evidence-gathering analyses, entropy dynamics, gradient-geometry diagnostics, and controls showing that position, predictive entropy, and loss normalization do not explain the observed asymmetry. Finally, a dynamic entropy-aware soft-reweighting intervention improves Qwen3-8B-Base from 34.39 to 37.40 held-out average in the strongest setting. These findings suggest that attention entropy reveals optimization-relevant structure in token-level RL signals, and that uniform token averaging can obscure meaningful heterogeneity in reasoning post-training.

*Fan Zhou,Tim Van de Cruys*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的CFG引导因子通常设为固定超参数，这在处理复杂或动态任务时导致可控性和生成质量的权衡不佳，尤其是在自然语言处理任务中，不同阶段最优的引导因子应随扩散过程变化而改变。

Method: 作者将CFG规模的选择建模为序列决策问题，利用强化学习，特别是Proximal Policy Optimization（PPO）算法，根据扩散状态动态选择每一步的引导因子。通过任务级别的奖励信号优化策略，实现自适应的引导轨迹。

Result: 在三个NLP受控生成任务上的实验表明，动态自适应调整引导因子的方案比传统固定因子的方案在可控性和生成质量之间达成了更佳的平衡。

Conclusion: 实验和策略分析显示，引导因子的动态调整能够产生有区分度且可解释的引导轨迹，因此将CFG规模视为动态控制变量而非静态设计，对提升生成模型表现具有重要意义。

Abstract: Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG) is a widely used mechanism for controlling diffusion-based generative models, yet its guidance scale is typically treated as a fixed hyperparameter throughout generation. This static design yields a suboptimal controllability and quality tradeoff, as the optimal degree of guidance varies across tasks and across different stages of the diffusion process, especially in NLP domain. We recast CFG scale selection as a sequential decision-making problem and propose to learn dynamic guidance trajectories via reinforcement learning. Specifically, we model the guidance scale as a discrete control action selected at each generation step based on the evolving diffusion state, and optimize a policy using Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) under task-level rewards. Experiments on three controlled NLP generation tasks using discrete diffusion language models demonstrate that adaptive guidance consistently achieves a better balance between controllability and generation quality than fixed-scale strategies. Further analysis of the learned policies reveals distinct and interpretable guidance trajectories across tasks, underscoring the importance of treating guidance as a dynamic control process rather than a static design choice.

### [218] [SimCT: Recovering Lost Supervision for Cross-Tokenizer On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07711)
*Jie Sun,Mao Zheng,Mingyang Song,Qiyong Zhong,Yilin Cheng,Bichuan Feng,Pengfei Liu,Junfeng Fang,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的跨分词器在策略蒸馏方法（SimCT），可以在教师模型和学生模型使用不同分词器时有效传递监督信号，显著提升感知性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在策略蒸馏（OPD）假设教师和学生模型分词一致，逐token对齐进行蒸馏。但在实际应用中，教师和学生模型往往采用异构分词器，直接导致许多教学信号在两者分词不一致处被丢弃，影响蒸馏效果。

Method: 作者提出SimCT方法，扩大监督空间：不仅利用共享token，还引入由两种分词器均能实现的短多token片段作为对齐和蒸馏基础，同时保持原有OPD损失不变。通过这种方式，将原本在分词不一致处会被忽略的监督信号纳入训练过程。

Result: 在三个数学推理和代码生成基准上的异构教师-学生对测试，SimCT均优于仅用共享token的OPD和典型跨分词蒸馏基线。消融实验进一步证明，性能提升源于恢复了大量被逐token对齐丢弃的监督信号。

Conclusion: SimCT作为一种简单有效的跨分词器在策略蒸馏方法，适用于教师-学生模型分词器不一致的场景，能增强模型间知识迁移，为未来相关模型压缩和知识蒸馏研究提供新思路。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) is a standard tool for transferring teacher behavior to a smaller student, but it implicitly assumes that teacher and student predictions are comparable token by token, an assumption that fails whenever the two models tokenize the same text differently. Under heterogeneous tokenizers, exact shared-token matching silently discards a large fraction of the teacher signal at precisely the positions where vocabularies disagree. We propose \textbf{\underline{Sim}ple \underline{C}ross-\underline{T}okenizer OPD (SimCT)}, which restores this signal by enlarging the supervision space: alongside shared tokens, SimCT compares teacher and student over short multi-token continuations that both tokenizers can realize, leaving the OPD loss form itself unchanged. We show that these units are the finest jointly tokenizable supervision interface, and that coarser alternatives remove teacher-student distinctions that are useful for on-policy learning. Across three heterogeneous teacher-student pairs on mathematical reasoning and code-generation benchmarks, SimCT shows consistent gains over shared-vocabulary OPD and representative cross-tokenizer baselines, with ablations confirming that the improvements come from recovering supervision discarded by exact shared-token matching. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/sunjie279/SimCT-}{https://github.com/sunjie279/SimCT-}.

</details>


### [219] [Memory-Efficient Looped Transformer: Decoupling Compute from Memory in Looped Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07721)
*Victor Conchello Vendrell,Arnau Padres Masdemont,Niccolò Grillo,Jordi Ros-Giralt,Arash Behboodi,Fabio Valerio Massoli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种内存高效的循环Transformer架构MELT，实现了与推理深度无关的内存消耗，并在循环语言模型任务上取得了与现有方法相媲美，且内存占用更低的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的循环LLM架构通过多次内嵌循环推理改进推理能力，但每增加一次迭代便增加一次KV缓存，导致内存消耗与推理步数线性增长，限制了模型扩展性。因此亟需解决推理深度与内存消耗耦合的问题。

Method: 提出MELT架构，用每层仅维护一个共享的KV缓存，并通过可学习门控机制在循环中更新该缓存，从而将推理深度与内存消耗解耦。为确保训练稳定与高效，提出两阶段chunk-wise训练法：先通过插值平滑模型过渡，再进行基于注意力的一致性蒸馏。

Result: 实验发现，基于Ouro参数微调的MELT在内存消耗与标准LLM相当、远低于传统循环LLM Ouro的前提下，在各种推理任务上性能更优。

Conclusion: MELT实现了常量内存的循环推理，在保持高推理性能的同时，大幅降低了内存需求，且仅需轻量后训练流程，极大提升了实际部署的可扩展性。

Abstract: Recurrent LLM architectures have emerged as a promising approach for improving reasoning, as they enable multi-step computation in the embedding space without generating intermediate tokens. Models such as Ouro perform reasoning by iteratively updating internal representations while retaining a standard Key-Value (KV) cache across iterations, causing memory consumption to grow linearly with reasoning depth. Consequently, increasing the number of reasoning iterations can lead to prohibitive memory usage, limiting the practical scalability of such architectures. In this work, we propose Memory-Efficient Looped Transformer (MELT), a novel architecture that decouples reasoning depth from memory consumption. Instead of using a standard KV cache per layer and loop, MELT maintains a single KV cache per layer that is shared across reasoning loops. This cache is updated over time via a learnable gating mechanism. To enable stable and efficient training under this architecture, we propose to train MELT using chunk-wise training in a two phase procedure: interpolated transition, followed by attention-aligned distillation, both from the LoopLM starting model to MELT. Empirically, we show that MELT models fine-tuned from pretrained Ouro parameters outperform standard LLMs of comparable size, while maintaining a memory footprint comparable to those models and dramatically smaller than Ouro's. Overall, MELT achieves constant-memory iterative reasoning without sacrificing LoopLM performance, using only a lightweight post-training procedure.

### [220] [SOD: Step-wise On-policy Distillation for Small Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07725)
*Qiyong Zhong,Mao Zheng,Mingyang Song,Xin Lin,Jie Sun,Houcheng Jiang,Xiang Wang,Junfeng Fang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于小语言模型工具集成推理的新型蒸馏方法SOD，在多个基准任务上有显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前小模型在多步工具推理中容易因模型容量有限和执行链失稳，导致推理效果不佳。现有强化学习方法奖励稀疏，基于OPD的密集监督却因推理链错误扩散而效果有限，需要新的方法增强蒸馏稳定性与泛化能力。

Method: 作者提出SOD（Step-wise On-policy Distillation）框架，根据每一步的师生分歧度动态调整蒸馏强度，高分歧步骤弱化老师信号，低分歧步骤保持高强度指导，从而减少级联错误并提升学习效果。

Result: 在数学、科学、代码等挑战性基准上，SOD方法在小模型上比第二优基线提升最高可达20.86%；其中0.6B规模的学生模型在AIME 2025上获得26.13%的成绩，展现了较好的推理迁移能力。

Conclusion: SOD框架有效缓解了小模型在工具推理场景下OPD监督失效的问题，推动小模型在复杂推理任务上的实用化进展。

Abstract: Tool-integrated reasoning (TIR) is difficult to scale to small language models due to instability in long-horizon tool interactions and limited model capacity. While reinforcement learning methods like group relative policy optimization provide only sparse outcome-level rewards. Recently, on-policy distillation (OPD) has gained popularity by supplying dense token-level supervision from a teacher on student-generated trajectories. However, our experiments indicate that applying OPD to TIR leads to a critical failure mode: erroneous tool calls tend to cascade across subsequent reasoning steps, progressively amplifying student-teacher divergence and rendering the teacher's token-level supervision increasingly unreliable. To address this, we propose SOD, a step-wise on-policy distillation framework for small language model agents, which adaptively reweights distillation strength at each step based on step-level divergence. Therefore, SOD can attenuate potentially misleading teacher signals in high-divergence regions while preserving dense guidance in well-aligned states. Experiments on challenging math, science, and code benchmarks show that SOD achieves up to 20.86% improvement over the second-best baseline. Notably, our 0.6B student achieves 26.13% on AIME 2025, demonstrating effective transfer of agentic reasoning to lightweight models. Our code is available at https://github.com/YoungZ365/SOD.

</details>

Abstract: This report benchmarks the performance of ENGINEERING Ingegneria Informatica S.p.A.'s EngGPT2MoE-16B-A3B LLM, a 16B parameter Mixture of Experts (MoE) model with 3B active parameters. Performance is investigated across a wide variety of representative benchmarks, and is compared against comparably-sized open-source MoE and dense models. In comparison with popular Italian models, namely FastwebMIIA-7B, Minerva-7B, Velvet-14B, and LLaMAntino-3-ANITA-8B, EngGPT2MoE-16B-A3B performs as well or better on international benchmarks: ARC-Challenge, GSM8K, AIME24, AIME25, MMLU, and HumanEval (HE). Compared with popular MoE models of comparable size, the new model reports higher values than DeepSeek-MoE-16B-Chat on all considered benchmarks. It has higher values than Moonlight-16B-A3B on HE, MMLU, AIME24, AIME25, GSM8K, and the 32k RULER setting, but lower on BFCL and some ARC and ITALIC settings. Finally it has lower values than GPT-OSS-20B on most benchmarks, including HE, MMLU, AIME24, AIME25, GSM8K, ARC, BFCL, and the RULER 32k. When compared with popular dense models, EngGPT2MoE-16B-A3B reports higher values on AIME24 and AIME25 than Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, Gemma-3-12b-it, and Ministral-3-8BInstruct-2512-BF16, but lower values on ITALIC, BFCL, and RULER with a 32k context. When performance is aggregated across all benchmark metrics, EngGPT2MoE-16B-A3B shows higher performance than the Italian models under evaluation while achieving lower results than some of the most performant international models, in particular GPT-5 nano and Qwen3-8B. Taken together, our findings find the new model to be a step forward for native Italian Large Language Models.

### [222] [TextLDM: Language Modeling with Continuous Latent Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07748)
*Jiaxiu Jiang,Jingjing Ren,Wenbo Li,Bo Wang,Haoze Sun,Yijun Yang,Jianhui Liu,Yanbing Zhang,Shenghe Zheng,Yuan Zhang,Haoyang Huang,Nan Duan,Wangmeng Zuo*

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新的语言生成模型TextLDM，将视觉领域成功的Diffusion Transformers方法迁移用于文本生成。通过在VAE潜空间及REPA对齐机制实现了高质量文本生成，性能与GPT-2相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前diffusion模型已将视觉生成统一用于图像与视频，下一步目标是将该统一架构扩展至文本生成，实现多模态的生成与理解。为此，需要解决如何获取高质量连续化文本潜表示的挑战。

Method: 提出TextLDM，借助基于Transformer的VAE，将离散文本token映射到连续潜空间，并通过REPA（与冻结的预训练语言模型对齐）提升表征。之后标准的Diffusion Transformer（DiT）在此潜空间内做flow matching，架构几乎不变。

Result: TextLDM在OpenWebText2从零训练，显著优于以往的扩散语言模型，并在相同设置下达到GPT-2表现。REPA机制显著提升下游生成质量。

Conclusion: 视觉领域DiT配方能够有效迁移到语言领域，为统一多模态生成和理解的扩散架构提供了实证基础和新的进展。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiT) trained with flow matching in a VAE latent space have unified visual generation across images and videos. A natural next step toward a single architecture for both generation (visual synthesis) and understanding (text generation) is to apply this framework to language modeling. We propose TextLDM, which transfers the visual latent diffusion recipe to text generation with minimal architectural modification. A Transformer-based VAE maps discrete tokens to continuous latents, enhanced by Representation Alignment (REPA) with a frozen pretrained language model to produce representations effective for conditional denoising. A standard DiT then performs flow matching in this latent space, identical in architecture to its visual counterpart. The central challenge we address is obtaining high-quality continuous text representations: we find that reconstruction fidelity alone is insufficient, and that aligning latent features with a pretrained language model via REPA is critical for downstream generation quality. Trained from scratch on OpenWebText2, TextLDM substantially outperforms prior diffusion language models and matches GPT-2 under the same settings. Our results establish that the visual DiT recipe transfers effectively to language, taking a concrete step toward unified diffusion architectures for multimodal generation and understanding.

### [223] [CktFormalizer: Autoformalization of Natural Language into Circuit Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07782)
*Jing Xiong,Qi Han,Chenchen Ding,He Xiao,Zunhai Su,Chaofan Tao,Ngai Wong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了CktFormalizer框架，通过在Lean 4中嵌入依赖类型硬件描述语言，改善LLM自动生成Verilog代码存在的硬件缺陷问题，实现更高的后端实现率和等效性机器证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM可根据自然语言自动生成Verilog硬件描述，但这类代码常因位宽不匹配、组合环路、不完整case等缺陷，虽然语法符合但合成或实际硬件运行时失败，急需更健全的生成及验证机制。

Method: 引入依赖类型HDL，嵌入Lean 4证明助理。利用Lean依赖类型：（i）类型检查器：将硬件位宽、覆盖率、无环等约束编码到类型系统，将缺陷转为编译期错误，指导修复；（ii）正确性隔离：保证编译后设计结构无易被后端工具忽略的隐性错误；（iii）证明助理：进行机器检验的功能等价性证明，超越有限状态机等传统验证能力。

Result: 在VerilogEval、RTLLM和ResBench三个基准（共262题）上，CktFormalizer生成电路的仿真通过率与直接生成Verilog的方法相当，但后端实现率显著提升：有95-100%的设计顺利完成综合、布局布线、DRC和LVS。闭环PPA优化阶段在验证等价性前提下，能带来高达35%面积和30%功耗的降低。

Conclusion: CktFormalizer框架能够将硬件生成过程中易被忽略的缺陷在编译和验证环节捕获，使得LLM生成的硬件代码实现性和可靠性均大幅提升，为自动化硬件设计提供了强有力的保障。

Abstract: LLMs can generate hardware descriptions from natural language specifications, but the resulting Verilog often contains width mismatches, combinational loops, and incomplete case logic that pass syntax checks yet fail in synthesis or silicon. We present CktFormalizer, a framework that redirects LLM-driven hardware generation through a dependently-typed HDL embedded in Lean 4. Lean serves three roles: (i) type checker:dependent types encode bit-width constraints, case coverage, and acyclicity, turning hardware defects into compile-time errors that guide iterative repair; (ii) correctness firewall:compiled designs are structurally free of defects that cause silent backend failures (the baseline loses 20% of correct designs during synthesis and routing; CktFormalizer preserves all of them); (iii) proof assistant:the agent constructs machine-checked equivalence proofs over arbitrary input sequences and parameterized widths, beyond the reach of bounded SMT-based checking. On VerilogEval (156 problems), RTLLM (50 problems), and ResBench (56 problems), CktFormalizer achieves simulation pass rates competitive with direct Verilog generation while delivering substantially higher backend realizability: 95--100% of compiled designs complete the full synthesis, place-and-route, DRC, and LVS flow. A closed-loop PPA optimization stage yields up to 35% area reduction and 30% power reduction through validated architecture exploration, with automated theorem proof ensuring that each optimized variant remains functionally equivalent to its formal specification.

### [224] [Chain-based Distillation for Effective Initialization of Variable-Sized Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07783)
*Boyu Shi,YiCheng Jiang,Chang Liu,Qiufeng Wang,Xu Yang,Xin Geng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的知识蒸馏方法——链式蒸馏（CBD），用于高效初始化不同规模的小语言模型，实现了大模型性能的高效迁移，显著提升了训练效率和下游性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）效果强，但部署成本高，小模型训练又耗时高昂；传统蒸馏方法面临对不同目标规模需要多次依赖大模型的问题，可扩展性差。

Method: 作者提出链式蒸馏（CBD），通过分阶段逐步从大模型向中间锚点模型知识转移，并在异构架构/词表下引入“桥接蒸馏”，支持不同结构间的知识迁移；不同规模模型可通过相邻锚点参数插值快速初始化，避免了重复推理大模型。

Result: 实验显示，CBD方法在效率和下游性能上均优于现有方案。例如，138M参数的小模型无需预训练即可超越同等规模从头训练模型，且在多架构、多词表条件下展现了通用性。

Conclusion: CBD极大提升了小模型初始化与蒸馏效率，同时能兼容不同模型规模、架构和词表，为资源受限环境下语言模型高效部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance but remain costly to deploy in resource-constrained settings. Training small language models (SLMs) from scratch is computationally expensive, while conventional knowledge distillation requires repeated access to large teachers for different target sizes, leading to poor scalability. To solve these problems, we propose \textbf{Chain-based Distillation (CBD)}, a scalable paradigm for efficiently initializing variable-sized language models. A sparse and limited sequence of intermediate models (called anchors) is constructed via stepwise distillation, forming a distillation chain that progressively transfers knowledge from the source LLMs. To support heterogeneous settings, we introduce \emph{bridge distillation} for cross-architecture and cross-vocabulary transfer. Models of variable sizes are initialized via parameter interpolation between adjacent anchors, eliminating repeated large teacher inference. Experiments show that the proposed method substantially improves efficiency and downstream performance. A 138M-parameter SLM without recovery pre-training, outperforms scratch-trained models on a 10B-token corpus on the specific task. CBD also demonstrates versatility in heterogeneous settings for initialize models with different architectures and vocabularies.

The dataset originally contains 732 rows and 191 fine-grained emotion labels; after cleaning, deduplication, and label remapping, 707 samples remain with an imbalanced distribution of 459 positive, 188 negative, and 60 neutral instances. Experimental results show that the Logistic Regression deployment model reaches 0.8028 accuracy, 0.8003 weighted F1, and 0.7276 macro F1, while project documentation reports a higher-accuracy but non-production MLP baseline. These findings indicate that careful preprocessing, interpretable feature engineering, and class balancing remain competitive for small Indonesian sentiment datasets, whereas the neural baseline is better treated as a comparative experiment than as the default deployment model.

### [226] [PolySQL: Scaling Text-to-SQL Evaluation Across SQL Dialects via Automated Backend Isomorphism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07796)
*Yotam Perlitz,Elad Venezian,Corentin Royer,Francesco Fusco,Andrea Giovannini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了PolySQL，一种无需查询转译即可跨SQL方言评测的双执行方法，并首次实现了大规模跨方言准确性研究。结果显示，基于SQLite的评测并不能代表其他方言，SQLite到其他方言的准确率平均下降10.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Text-to-SQL基准多仅支持SQLite，导致其他数据库方言的模型表现评估存在巨大空缺，且人工或工具的查询转译方案成本高或效果差，亟需新方法解决跨SQL方言评测难题。

Method: 提出PolySQL，一种基于对比标准化执行结果的双执行方法，无需人工转译查询，能覆盖全部查询类型。并构建包含三套数据集的评测框架，实现自动化大规模方言对比。

Result: PolySQL相比转译法具有更高评估准确性和完整查询覆盖。实验发现，从SQLite到其他SQL方言模型准确率平均下降10.1%，且主因是逻辑误差（61%），而非语法差异（8%）。

Conclusion: 本文证明了仅使用SQLite评测方法的局限性，并提供了高可靠性的跨方言评测工具，对于推动Text-to-SQL模型的方言泛化和公平性研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: SQL dialects vary in syntax, types, and functions across database engines. Text-to-SQL benchmarks, however, predominantly support only SQLite. This creates a critical evaluation gap: cross-dialect evaluation reveals weak per-query agreement (Cohen's ), showing that SQLite performance is an unreliable proxy for other dialects. Yet such evaluation remains prohibitively difficult: existing approaches either require expensive manual query transpilation or rely on tools that often fail on complex SQL. To close this gap, we introduce PolySQL, a novel dual-execution method that eliminates the need for query transpilation by comparing normalized execution results. Notably, our approach achieves higher evaluation fidelity than query transpilation with 100% query coverage. PolySQL comprises three datasets, enabling the first large-scale cross-dialect study. Our study reveals a 10.1% average accuracy drop from SQLite to other dialects and identifies a significant dialect difficulty hierarchy. We find this degradation stems from logical rather than syntactic errors (61% vs. 8%). We release our framework code and leaderboard to enable rigorous dialect-robust evaluation.

### [227] [Beyond Confidence: Rethinking Self-Assessments for Performance Prediction in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07806)
*Sree Bhattacharyya,Samarth Khanna,Leona Chen,Lucas Craig,Tharun Dilliraj,James Z. Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种多维度自我评估方法，通过六个评价维度提升大语言模型（LLM）失败预测的可靠性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LLM对于自我评估多依赖单一的置信度，但这种方法常常过于乐观且不稳定。受认知评价理论启发，作者希望通过引入更多评估维度改善LLM的自我判断能力，以提升实际应用中的可靠性与安全性。

Method: 基于人类心理学中的认知评价理论，将自我评估分解为六个维度（包括努力、能力等），并与传统置信度对比，通过跨12个模型、38个任务和八个领域的数据实验，分析各评价维度对模型失败预测的表现。

Result: 与置信度相比，反映能力相关的维度（如努力与能力）在大多数情况下拥有更好的预测性能，尤其是努力维度对于推理类任务表现更优，而且随着模型规模变化更为稳定。情感维度预警性有限。

Conclusion: 结构化的多维自我评估能显著提升语言模型在实际应用环境下的可靠性和安全性，尤其不同任务下应侧重不同评估维度，对未来模型自我评估体系建设具有指导意义。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in settings where reliable self-assessment is critical. Assessing model reliability has evolved from using probabilistic correctness estimates to, more recently, eliciting verbalized confidence. Confidence, however, has been shown to be an inconsistent and overoptimistic predictor of model correctness. Drawing on cognitive appraisal theory, a framework from human psychology that decomposes self-evaluation into multiple components, we propose a multidimensional perspective on model self-assessment. We elicit six appraisal-based dimensions of self-assessment, alongside confidence, and evaluate their utility for predicting model failure across 12 LLMs and 38 tasks spanning eight domains. We find that competence-related appraisal dimensions, particularly effort and ability, consistently match or outperform confidence across most settings. Effort additionally yields less overoptimistic estimates that remain stable across model sizes. In contrast, affective dimensions provide marginally predictive signals. Furthermore, the most informative dimension varies systematically with task characteristics: effort is most predictive for reasoning-intensive tasks, while ability and confidence dominate on retrieval-oriented tasks. Broadly, our findings indicate that structured multidimensional self-assessment is a promising approach to improving the reliability and safety of language model deployment across diverse real-world settings.

</details>

### [229] [SCENE: Recognizing Social Norms and Sanctioning in Group Chats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07823)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在多方聊天环境下能否识别和适应隐性行为规范并未被充分探究，因此需要一个专门的评估基准。

Method: 设计SCENE基准，生成具有隐藏规范的非角色扮演多方聊天场景，由剧本化角色引导目标模型可能违反规范，并在违规时给予社交制裁，建立两类针对社交适应能力的行为评估指标。

Result: 对六款前沿及开放权重模型在SCENE上的表现进行了评测，发现Claude Opus 4.7和Gemini 3.1 Pro对隐性规范的适应能力明显优于其他开放权重模型。

Conclusion: SCENE为大语言模型社交能力的动态、互动式评测提供了基准，有助于推动该方向的研究。

Abstract: Online group chats are social spaces with implicit behavior patterns that, when broken, are often met with social sanctioning from the group. The ability and willingness of LLM-based agents to recognize and adapt to these norms remains mostly unexplored. We introduce SCENE, a social-interaction benchmark focused on implicit norms and social sanctioning in multi-party chat. SCENE generates plausible non-roleplay scenarios with scripted personas that follow a hidden norm, create opportunities for the subject agent to violate it, and sanction breaches when they occur. We further propose behavioral evaluation metrics for two functional adaptation abilities: responsiveness to negative sanctioning, and adapting norm from peers behavior. We evaluate six frontier and open-weight models on SCENE. Our results show that Claude Opus 4.7 and Gemini 3.1 Pro adapt to implicit norms significantly more than the evaluated open-weight models. SCENE contributes one benchmark in the direction of recent calls for dynamic, interactional evaluation of LLM social capabilities.

</details>


### [230] [Measuring and Mitigating the Distributional Gap Between Real and Simulated User Behaviors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07847)
*Shuhaib Mehri,Philippe Laban,Sumuk Shashidhar,Marwa Abdulhai,Sergey Levine,Michel Galley,Dilek Hakkani-Tür*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新方法，用于衡量AI用户模拟器与真实用户行为分布之间的差距，并系统评测了24个基于LLM的用户模拟器，揭示了其与真实用户存在显著行为分布差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前用户模拟器在AI助手交互训练与评估中作用越来越大，但现有方法虽能生成类人回复，却尚不清楚能否捕获真实用户行为的广泛异质分布。因此，有必要对模拟器与真实用户行为的分布差异进行系统化分析。

Method: 作者提出了一套评价流程：首先从真实和模拟对话中提取用户行为表征，再通过聚类量化为离散分布，最后计算分布间的距离。方法还辅以人类研究与消融实验验证。

Result: 对24种LLM用户模拟器在编程和写作任务中的表现进行了首次系统评测。发现大多数模拟器行为相似，但与真实用户存在较大分布差异，少数模拟器表现出独特行为。多模拟器组合作为行为互补手段可更好逼近真实用户分布。进一步，对行为模式进行TF-IDF分析，可解释哪些行为被模拟器覆盖、遗漏或误判。

Conclusion: AI用户模拟器与真实用户在行为分布上存在显著差异，单一模拟器难以全面覆盖真实行为，未来应关注多模拟器互补和行为多样性的提升，同时用分布度量手段进行客观评价。

Abstract: As user simulators are increasingly used for interactive training and evaluation of AI assistants, it is essential that they represent the diverse behaviors of real users. While existing works train user simulators to generate human-like responses, whether they capture the broad and heterogeneous distribution of real user behaviors remains an open question. In this work, we introduce a method to measure the distributional gap between real and simulated user behaviors, validated through a human study and ablations. Given a dataset of real and simulated conversations, our method extracts representations of user behavior from each conversation, quantizes them into discrete distributions via clustering, then computes divergence metrics. We provide the first systematic evaluation of 24 LLM-based user simulators on coding and writing tasks, and reveal a large distributional gap from real users that varies across model families, scales, and behavioral facets. Pairwise comparisons show that most simulators behave similarly, while a few stand apart. Combining behaviorally complementary simulators brings the resulting distribution closer to real users compared to either simulator on its own. Finally, a TF-IDF analysis of the clusters surfaces interpretable patterns of behaviors that simulators capture, miss, and hallucinate.

### [231] [MatryoshkaLoRA: Learning Accurate Hierarchical Low-Rank Representations for LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07850)
*Ionut-Vlad Modoranu,Mher Safaryan,Dan Alistarh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的低秩适应微调方法MatryoshkaLoRA，提高了大型深度学习模型微调的效率和精度，并支持动态秩选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当今深度学习模型参数规模极大，微调需要大量计算资源。虽然低秩适应（LoRA）方法可以高效微调，但其秩r需事先设定且要通过网格搜索确定，效率低下。现有自适应秩方案（如DyLoRA）存在梯度信息传播不充分导致高秩效果差、数据利用率不高等问题。

Method: 作者提出MatryoshkaLoRA，在LoRA结构内部插入一个精心设计的对角矩阵P，使各层级的子秩都能有效获得梯度信息。该框架可通过改变P还原为LoRA与DyLoRA，并支持动态选秩。作者还提出了AURAC指标，用于系统评估低秩适配器在不同秩下的效果。

Result: 相比现有方法，MatryoshkaLoRA能在各秩下取得更准确的低秩表示和更优的效率-效果平衡，在多组测试数据上均优于主流方法。

Conclusion: MatryoshkaLoRA为大模型高效微调提供了一种通用且高效的框架，在保持性能的同时显著提升了秩自适应能力和数据利用效率。

Abstract: With the rise in scale for deep learning models to billions of parameters, the computational cost of fine-tuning remains a significant barrier to deployment. While Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) has become the standard for parameter-efficient fine-tuning, the need to set a predefined, static rank $r$ requires exhaustive grid searches to balance efficiency and performance. Existing rank-adaptive solutions such as DyLoRA mitigate this by sampling ranks during the training from a predefined distribution. However, they often yield sub-optimal results at higher ranks due to lack of consistent gradient signals across the full hierarchy of ranks, thus making these methods data-inefficient. In this paper, we propose MatryoshkaLoRA, a general, Matryoshka-inspired training framework for LoRA that learns accurate hierarchical low-rank representations by inserting a fixed, carefully crafted diagonal matrix $P$ between the existing LoRA adapters to scale their sub-ranks accordingly. By introducing this simple modification, our general framework recovers LoRA and DyLoRA only by changing $P$ and ensures all sub-ranks embed the available gradient information efficiently. Our MatryoshkaLoRA supports dynamic rank selection with minimal degradation in accuracy. We further propose Area Under the Rank Accuracy Curve (AURAC), a metric that consistently evaluates the performance of hierarchical low-rank adapters. Our results demonstrate that MatryoshkaLoRA learns more accurate hierarchical low-rank representations than prior rank-adaptive approaches and achieves superior accuracy-performance trade-offs across ranks on the evaluated datasets. Our code is available at https://github.com/IST-DASLab/MatryoshkaLoRA.

</details>


### [232] [Beyond "I cannot fulfill this request": Alleviating Rigid Rejection in LLMs via Label Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07883)
*Ying Zhang,Congyu Qiao,Xin Geng,Ning Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出LANCE方法，通过标签增强和细粒度拒绝策略，提升大语言模型（LLM）拒绝有害请求时的自然性和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在安全对齐时，常用“一刀切”式的回绝模板，导致与用户互动呆板、不自然。研究动机是如何使LLM在拒绝有害请求的同时，保持回应的自然和灵活性，优化用户体验。

Method: 提出LANCE方法，利用变分推断进行标签增强，对多种拒绝类别分布进行预测，生成细粒度的拒绝分布。通过这些分布为精化模型提供“文本梯度”，帮助模型精确中和提示中的有害元素，从而输出安全且自然的回应，避免僵硬回绝。

Result: 实验表明，LANCE大幅减轻了僵硬拒绝问题，在安全性的前提下，响应的有用性和自然性均显著优于现有基线模型。

Conclusion: LANCE能在保障安全的前提下，实现LLM有害请求拒绝的灵活性和自然性，为未来复杂对话系统的安全与交互体验提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) rely on safety alignment to obey safe requests while refusing harmful ones. However, traditional refusal mechanisms often lead to "rigid rejection," where a general template (e.g., "I cannot fulfill this request") indiscriminately triggers refusals and severely undermines the naturalness of interactions between humans and LLMs. To address this issue, LANCE is proposed in this paper to ensure safe yet flexible and natural responses via label enhancement. Specifically, LANCE employs variational inference to perform label enhancement, predicting a continuous distribution across multiple rejection categories. These fine-grained rejection distributions provide multi-way textual gradients for a refinement model to neutralize the hazardous elements in the prompt, so that the LLMs could generate safe responses that avoid rigid rejections while preserving the naturalness of interactions. Experiments demonstrate that LANCE significantly alleviates the rigid rejection problem while maintaining high security standards, significantly outperforming existing baseline models in terms of helpfulness and naturalness of responses.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI评审系统的评估方法偏重与人类评审内容的重叠，而忽视了其正确性和完整性。人类评审未必覆盖全部要点，且有误判，作为金标准存在问题，亟需新的评估方法。

Method: 1）建立类别细分的基准子集，在缺失对应领域人类评审时跳过评估，提高评测的完整性。2）利用审稿人-作者-主审讨论过程作为专家标注，过滤不可靠的评审，以提升正确性。3）引入CoCoReviewBench，收集自ICLR和NeurIPS的3900篇论文，支持细粒度的AI评审系统评价。

Abstract: Despite the rapid development of AI reviewers, evaluating such systems remains challenging: metrics favor overlap with human reviews over correctness. However, since human reviews often cover only a subset of salient issues and sometimes contain mistakes, they are unreliable as gold references. To address this, we build category-specific benchmark subsets and skip evaluation when the corresponding human reviews are missing to strengthen Completeness. We also leverage reviewer--author--meta-review discussions as expert annotations and filter unreliable reviews accordingly to strengthen Correctness. Finally, we introduce CoCoReviewBench, which curates 3,900 papers from ICLR and NeurIPS to enable reliable and fine-grained evaluation of AI reviewers. Analysis shows that AI reviewers remain limited in correctness and are prone to hallucinations, and highlights reasoning models as more effective reviewers, motivating further directions for improving AI reviewers. Benchmarks and models are available at https://github.com/hexuandeng/CoCoReviewBench.

### [234] [How Value Induction Reshapes LLM Behaviour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07925)
*Arnav Arora,Natalie Schluter,Katherine Metcalf,Maartje ter Hoeve*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大语言模型中注入特定价值观对模型行为的多重影响，发现不仅会增强目标价值观，还会影响其他行为、安全性和语言表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来对大语言模型的微调常聚焦于灌输比如好奇心、开放性、同理心、助人、无害和诚实等行为或价值观，以提高用户体验和模型安全性。但作者关注到，价值观彼此复杂关联，渗透一种可能会并发影响其他类型行为，同时有可能引发模型变得更讨好用户甚至上瘾，带来副作用。本文希望系统分析这些副作用。

Method: 作者用精心挑选的偏好数据子集对模型进行特定价值观的微调，通过定量实验评估这种“价值注入”对其他价值表现、安全性、拟人化语言以及典型问答能力的影响。

Result: （1）灌输一种价值观会让模型表达出更多相关或对立的价值观；（2）正向价值的注入可以增强模型的安全性；（3）所有类型的价值注入都会使模型产生更多拟人化（易讨好/奉承）语言表现。

Conclusion: 注入不同价值观虽可提升特定目标，但不可避免地改变了其他维度的行为和表现，尤其是提升了模型“讨好”或“奉承”特性。设计微调策略时需权衡这些副作用。

Abstract: Conversational Large Language Models are post-trained on language that expresses specific behavioural traits, such as curiosity, open-mindedness, and empathy, and values, such as helpfulness, harmlessness, and honesty. This is done to increase utility, ensure safety, and improve the experience of the people interacting with the model. However, values are complex and inter-related -- inducing one could modify behaviour on another. Further, inducing certain values can make models more addictive or sycophantic through language used in the generations, with a potential detrimental effect on the user. We investigate these and other unintended effects of value induction into models. We fine-tune models using curated value subsets of existing preference datasets, measuring the impact of value induction on expression of other values, model safety, anthropomorphic language, and various QA benchmarks. We find that (i) inducing values leads to expression of other related, and sometimes contrastive values, (ii) inducing positive values increases safety, and (iii) all values increase anthropomorphic language use, making models more validating and sycophantic.

</details>


### [235] [Ask Early, Ask Late, Ask Right: When Does Clarification Timing Matter for Long-Horizon Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07937)
*Anmol Gulati,Hariom Gupta,Elias Lumer,Sahil Sen,Vamse Kumar Subbiah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“强制注入”框架，系统研究AI智能体流程中在不同时间点澄清不完整指令的价值，并揭示最佳澄清时机与缺失信息类型相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前长周期AI智能体在面对不完整信息和指令时，缺乏对“澄清”最佳时机的定量研究，现有理论框架缺少实证基础，导致实际模型或过度澄清或完全不提问，影响任务完成表现。

Method: 作者设计了一个强制注入框架，在智能体执行流程特定阶段（覆盖目标、输入、约束、上下文四类信息）强制提供澄清，并在三套基准Agent、四个最前沿模型下，对84种任务变体进行了多次实验（6000+轮）；另外还分析了300个无剧本实际交互场景。

Result: 实验发现，澄清的价值因信息类型而异：目标相关澄清在执行早期（前10%）后几乎无效，而输入相关信息则在大约一半流程内仍有价值；任何类型若在流程后半段再澄清，效果甚至不如从不澄清。模型间的时序表现受任务内在属性影响较大。当前主流模型均未能把握最佳澄清窗口，表现为过度或缺乏澄清。

Conclusion: 首次定量描绘出AI智能体澄清价值的时序特性和任务内在属性相关性，为理论框架和实际系统中的时序敏感澄清策略提供了明确的实证依据。代码与数据将开放。

Abstract: Long-horizon AI agents execute complex workflows spanning hundreds of sequential actions, yet a single wrong assumption early on can cascade into irreversible errors. When instructions are incomplete, the agent must decide not only whether to ask for clarification but when, and no prior work measures how clarification value changes over the course of execution. We introduce a forced-injection framework that provides ground-truth clarifications at controlled points in the agent's trajectory across four information dimensions (goal, input, constraint, context), three agent benchmarks, and four frontier models (three per benchmark; one on a single benchmark only; 84 task variants; 6,000+ runs). Counter to the common intuition that "earlier is always better," we find that the value of clarification depends sharply on what information is missing: goal clarification loses nearly all value after 10% of execution (pass@3 drops from 0.78 to baseline), while input clarification retains value through roughly 50%. Deferring any clarification type past mid-trajectory degrades performance below never asking at all. Cross-model Kendall tau correlations (0.78-0.87 among models sharing identical task coverage; 0.34-0.67 across the full 4-model panel) confirm these timing profiles are substantially task-intrinsic. A complementary study of 300 unscripted sessions reveals that no current frontier model asks within the empirically optimal window, with strategies ranging from over-asking (52% of sessions) to never asking at all. These empirical demand curves provide the quantitative foundation that existing theoretical frameworks require but have lacked, and establish concrete design targets for timing-aware clarification policies. Code and data will be publicly released.

</details>


### [236] [GLiGuard: Schema-Conditioned Classification for LLM Safeguard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07982)
*Urchade Zaratiana,Mary Newhauser,George Hurn-Maloney,Ash Lewis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GLiGuard提出了一种低参数、高效率的内容审核模型，用于大模型输出的实时安全性检测，在准确率和延迟上优于现有大参数模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型内容审核主要采用自回归解码器（7B-27B参数），把分类问题当作文本生成，导致高延迟与多维度评估的扩展性差。需要一种可在多安全维度下实时、高效扩展的内容审核方法。

Method: 作者提出GLiGuard, 基于GLiNER2改造的0.3B参数双向编码器。通过在输入序列中引入结构化的任务定义与标签语义（schema-conditioned输入），能在一次非自回归前向传递中同时检测多个安全维度、细致危害分类及越狱策略。

Result: 在九个主流安全基准集上，GLiGuard的F1成绩接近7B-27B参数的解码器型guard模型，但模型参数只有其1/23到1/90，且推理吞吐量提升16倍、延迟降低17倍。

Conclusion: 轻量双向编码器可以显著降低推理成本的同时，保持与超大模型相近的审核准确率，为大模型安全性部署提供高效可扩展的新方案。

Abstract: Ensuring safe, policy-compliant outputs from large language models requires real-time content moderation that can scale across multiple safety dimensions. However, state-of-the-art guardrail models rely on autoregressive decoders with 7B--27B parameters, reformulating what is fundamentally a classification problem as sequential text generation, a design choice that incurs high latency and scales poorly to multi-aspect evaluation. In this work, we introduce \textbf{GLiGuard}, a 0.3B-parameter schema-conditioned bidirectional encoder adapted from GLiNER2 for LLM content moderation. The key idea is to encode task definitions and label semantics directly into the input sequence as structured token schemas, enabling simultaneous evaluation of prompt safety, response safety, refusal detection, 14 fine-grained harm categories, and 11 jailbreak strategies in a single non-autoregressive forward pass. This schema-conditioned design lets supported task and label blocks be composed directly in the input schema at inference time. Across nine established safety benchmarks, GLiGuard achieves F1 scores competitive with 7B--27B decoder-based guards despite being 23--90$\times$ smaller, while delivering up to 16$\times$ higher throughput and 17$\times$ lower latency. These results suggest that compact bidirectional encoders can approach the accuracy of much larger guard models while drastically reducing inference cost. Code and models are available at https://github.com/fastino-ai/GLiGuard.

</details>


### [237] [Tool Calling is Linearly Readable and Steerable in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07990)
*Zekun Wu,Ze Wang,Seonglae Cho,Yufei Yang,Adriano Koshiyama,Sahan Bulathwela,Maria Perez-Ortiz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI模型（如Gemma、Qwen、Llama等）在调用工具时，对所选工具的内部表示方式与可控性。作者发现，通过操作模型内部状态，可以高精度地控制和预测工具选择，并分析了出错概率的可预测性及其内部机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实应用中，AI代理选择错误工具往往直到执行环节才暴露（如发错邮件、错过会议），缺乏对错误的即时预警和干预机制。理解模型对于工具身份选择的内部表示规律，有望在决策前就精准预警和纠正错误，提高AI系统的安全性与实用性。

Method: 作者对12个不同规模的指令微调大模型进行探测，分析模型内部激活与工具选择的关系。采用均值差分、激活修补等方法，探索调整内部状态对选择行为的因果影响，并用向量投影等手段定位关键神经元。论文还通过与不同领域/同主题多工具任务测试，进一步排除话题相关性偏差。

Result: 实验表明，通过简单地对比工具间内部平均激活便可高精度“切换”模型选择工具（4B规模及以上模型准确率达93-100%）；且工具选择强度的内部差异能够有效预判错误（小差距样本出错率激增）。工具信号大量集中在输出层首token及少量注意力头。基础模型虽还不能生成正确工具，但内部已“记住”正确答案（Cosine准确率远超基线），表明预训练形成表征、微调连接表征与输出。

Conclusion: AI大模型在工具选择决策上内部表征充分且可控，通过激活分析与干预不仅可以精准修改选择，还可提前发现错误。这为AI安全、自动化异常预警、可解释性等应用提供了新方法，但多轮复杂代理任务仍较脆弱，需要后续继续探索。

Abstract: When a tool-calling agent picks the wrong tool, the failure is invisible until execution: the email gets sent, the meeting gets missed. Probing 12 instruction-tuned models across Gemma 3, Qwen 3, Qwen 2.5, and Llama 3.1 (270M to 27B), we find the identity of the chosen tool is linearly readable and steerable inside the model. Adding the mean-difference between two tools' average internal activations switches which tool the model selects at 77-100% accuracy on name-only single-turn prompts (93-100% at 4B+), and the JSON arguments that follow autoregressively match the new tool's schema, so flipping the name is enough. The same per-tool means also flag likely errors before they happen: on Gemma 3 12B and 27B, queries where the gap between the top-1 and top-2 tool is smallest produce 14-21x more wrong calls than queries with the largest gap. The causal effect concentrates along one direction, the row of the output layer that produces the target tool's first token: a unit vector along it at matched magnitude already reaches 93-100%, while what is left over leaves the choice almost untouched. Activation patching localises this to a small set of mid- and late-layer attention heads, and a within-topic probe across 14 same-domain $τ$-bench airline tools reaches top-1 61-89% across five 4B-14B models, ruling out the reading that we are just moving the model along a topic axis. Even base models encode the right tool before they can emit it: cosine readout from the internal state recovers 69-82% on BFCL while base generation reaches only 2-10%, suggesting pretraining forms the representation and instruction tuning later wires it to the output. We measure tool identity selection and JSON schema correctness in single-turn fixed-menu settings; multi-turn agentic transfer is more fragile and is discussed in Limitations.

</details>


### [238] [Fast Byte Latent Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08044)
*Julie Kallini,Artidoro Pagnoni,Tomasz Limisiewicz,Gargi Ghosh,Luke Zettlemoyer,Christopher Potts,Xiaochuang Han,Srinivasan Iyer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了Byte Latent Transformer (BLT) 及其一系列高效生成方法，极大提升了字节级语言模型的生成速度，并显著降低了内存带宽消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然字节级语言模型在性能上已能媲美基于token的模型，并摆脱了子词词表依赖，但它们的逐字节自回归生成方式导致推理十分缓慢，制约了实际应用。作者希望通过改进训练与推理流程，突破这一速度瓶颈。

Method: 本文主要提出三种新方法：（1）BLT Diffusion（BLT-D），结合block-wise扩散目标与传统的下一字节预测损失，从而每步可并行生成多个字节，减少前向计算次数；（2）BLT 自我推测（BLT-S），允许本地解码器越过预设边界草拟字节，通过一次全模型前向验证，提高质量；（3）BLT Diffusion+Verification（BLT-DV），在扩散生成后添加自回归验证步骤，提升生成准确性。

Result: 所有提出的方法在生成任务中的内存带宽消耗均比原BLT模型低50%以上，不同方案在生成质量和速度间具备不同权衡与优势。

Conclusion: 本研究显著提升了字节级语言模型实际应用的可行性，提出的各类高效方法有效突破了自回归生成速度瓶颈，为字节级语言模型的大规模落地扫清关键障碍。

Abstract: Recent byte-level language models (LMs) match the performance of token-level models without relying on subword vocabularies, yet their utility is limited by slow, byte-by-byte autoregressive generation. We address this bottleneck in the Byte Latent Transformer (BLT) through new training and generation techniques. First, we introduce BLT Diffusion (BLT-D), a new model and our fastest BLT variant, trained with an auxiliary block-wise diffusion objective alongside the standard next-byte prediction loss. This enables an inference procedure that generates multiple bytes in parallel per decoding step, substantially reducing the number of forward passes required to generate a sequence. Second, we propose two extensions inspired by speculative decoding that trade some of this speed for higher generation quality: BLT Self-speculation (BLT-S), in which BLT's local decoder continues generating past its normal patch boundaries to draft bytes, which are then verified with a single full-model forward pass; and BLT Diffusion+Verification (BLT-DV), which augments BLT-D with an autoregressive verification step after diffusion-based generation. All methods may achieve an estimated memory-bandwidth cost over 50% lower than BLT on generation tasks. Each approach offers its own unique advantages, together removing key barriers to the practical use of byte-level LMs.

</details>

### [240] [Accurate and Efficient Statistical Testing for Word Semantic Breadth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08048)
*Yo Ehara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于Householder反射对齐的置换检验方法，用于更准确地比较词语语义广度，显著降低了I类错误，并在GPU实现下大幅提升了计算速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统利用token向量分散度来衡量词语语义广度的方法存在误判风险，不同词语的语义方向差异可能被误认为语义广度差异，导致统计显著性测试失真，增加I类错误。作者希望找到一种方法，能有效区分真实语义广度差异与语义方向差异。

Method: 作者提出用Householder反射将比较的两个词的token向量云的均值对齐，使方向性误差最小化后再进行置换检验。同时，提出一种面向GPU的算法加速线性代数运算与批量置换操作。

Result: 这种对齐方案可将I类错误率降低32.5%，并在检验广度差异的灵敏度保持不变的前提下，GPU实现较CPU提速23倍。

Conclusion: Householder对齐置换检验能更加准确、可靠地比较词语的语义广度，避免方向性差异带来的误判，同时具备高效的计算性能，适于大规模词汇分析任务。

Abstract: Measuring the breadth of a word's meaning, or its spread across contexts, has become feasible with contextualized token embeddings. A word type can be represented as a cloud of token vectors, with dispersion-based statistics serving as proxies for contextual diversity (Nagata and Tanaka-Ishii, ACL2025). These measurements are useful for deciding appropriate sense distinctions when constructing thesauri and domain-specific dictionaries. However, when comparing the breadth of two word types, naive hypothesis testing on dispersion can be misleading: differences in semantic direction can masquerade as dispersion differences, inflating Type-I error and yielding "statistically significant" outcomes even when there is no true breadth difference. This is problematic because significance testing should distinguish genuine effects from incidental fluctuations in small-difference regimes. We propose a Householder-aligned permutation test to isolate dispersion differences from directional differences. Our method applies a single Householder reflection to align the mean directions of the two word types and then performs a permutation test on the aligned token clouds, yielding calibrated, non-parametric p-values. For practicality, we introduce a GPU-oriented implementation that batches permutations and linear algebra operations. Empirically, our alignment reduced Type-I error by 32.5% while preserving sensitivity to genuine breadth differences, and achieved a 23x speedup over the CPU baseline.

</details>


### [241] [CA-SQL: Complexity-Aware Inference Time Reasoning for Text-to-SQL via Exploration and Compute Budget Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08057)
*James Petullo,Nianwen Xue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Text-to-SQL任务在难度较高的BIRD基准测试上表现不佳，主要原因在于解空间探索不足，难以发现高质量的候选查询。本研究旨在解决这一难题，提升现有大语言模型（LLM）的复杂推理能力。

Method: 提出CA-SQL流程：1）根据任务难度动态调整候选解生成的广度；2）设计基于进化搜索理念的自定义prompt初始化方法，增强LLM的探索性；3）采用新颖的投票机制从候选解中选择最优解。

Result: 实验显示，仅用GPT-4o-mini模型即在BIRD基准"challenging"等级任务上取得51.72%的SOTA分数，超越采用更大模型的其他方法。总体上，在BIRD开发集达到了61.06%的执行准确率和68.77%的Soft F1分数。

Conclusion: 通过难度感知的动态探索和高效的候选筛选技术，CA-SQL显著提升了LLM在复杂Text-to-SQL任务上的性能，在资源有限情况下也能取得强竞争力，为后续相关研究提供了价值借鉴。

Abstract: While recent advancements in inference-time learning have improved LLM reasoning on Text-to-SQL tasks, current solutions still struggle to perform well on the most challenging tasks in the Bird-Bench (BIRD) benchmark. This is due to inadequate solution space exploration, which is necessary to uncover promising candidate queries that can be further refined to produce the correct output. To address this challenge, we introduce CA-SQL, a novel Text-to-SQL pipeline that utilizes the estimated difficulty of a task to dynamically scale the breadth of the exploration for generating solution candidates. In addition, we use a custom prompt seeding method, based on principles of evolutionary search, to further elicit exploratory behavior from the base LLM and a novel voting method to select the best candidate solution at the end of the search. Experiments demonstrate that our solution achieves a state-of-the-art score of 51.72% on the "challenging" tier of BIRD development set problems, using only GPT-4o-mini, out-performing other in-context learning approaches, even those that leverage larger models. Overall, our method attains a competitive 61.06% execution accuracy and 68.77% Soft F1 score on the BIRD development dataset.

### [242] [The Memory Curse: How Expanded Recall Erodes Cooperative Intent in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08060)
*Jiayuan Liu,Tianqin Li,Shiyi Du,Xin Luo,Haoxuan Zeng,Emanuel Tewolde,Tai Sing Lee,Tonghan Wang,Carl Kingsford,Vincent Conitzer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 扩展LLM上下文窗口本被认为是能力提升，但在多智能体博弈中反而有时破坏了合作，这种现象被称为“记忆诅咒”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然长上下文窗口被广泛认为能增强模型表现，但作者关注其在多智能体博弈（如囚徒困境等）中的实际作用，怀疑记忆扩展未必总是积极提升。

Method: 作者对7种LLM、4个社会博弈游戏、500轮实验进行了对照分析，通过溯因推理、词汇分析、定向微调、记忆内容替换、链式推理消融等方法，系统研究扩展记忆窗口对合作性的影响及其机制。

Result: 记忆窗口扩展在28组实验中有18组破坏了多智能体合作。词汇分析发现这与前瞻性意图减弱有关，不是模型变“多疑”。定向微调和记忆‘消毒’实验显示，触发合作瓦解的关键是记忆内容。链式推理曾加剧合作崩坏。

Conclusion: 记忆长度和内容会显著影响LLM多智能体行为。上下文非单纯增强协作，反而可能引发合作性崩坏，提示需关注推理结构与记忆管理对智能体群体行为的影响。

Abstract: Context window expansion is often treated as a straightforward capability upgrade for LLMs, but we find it systematically fails in multi-agent social dilemmas. Across 7 LLMs and 4 games over 500 rounds, expanding accessible history degrades cooperation in 18 of 28 model--game settings, a pattern we term the memory curse. We isolate the underlying mechanism through three analyses. First, lexical analysis of 378,000 reasoning traces associates this breakdown with eroding forward-looking intent rather than rising paranoia. We validate this using targeted fine-tuning as a cognitive probe: a LoRA adapter trained exclusively on forward-looking traces mitigates the decay and transfers zero-shot to distinct games. Second, memory sanitization holds prompt length fixed while replacing visible history with synthetic cooperative records, which restores cooperation substantially, proving the trigger is memory content, not length alone. Finally, ablating explicit Chain-of-Thought reasoning often reduces the collapse, showing that deliberation paradoxically amplifies the memory curse. Together, these results recast memory as an active determinant of multi-agent behavior: longer recall can either destabilize or support cooperation depending on the reasoning patterns it elicits.

</details>

*Shuhang Lin,Chuhao Zhou,Xiao Lin,Zihan Dong,Kuan Lu,Zhencan Peng,Jie Yin,Dimitris N. Metaxas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CPR的可信知识图谱问答（KGQA）方法，显著提升了答案覆盖率和预测集紧凑性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KGQA方法虽能实现可解释推理，但在答案的置信覆盖率上缺乏保障，传统的保形预测（CP）应用受限于校准可靠性差和分数辨别性不足，导致预测集过大或者置信度无法满足要求。

Method: 提出的CPR方法包括两个创新点：1）在路径级别分数上做查询级别的保形校准，保持样本交换性，生成具有统计保证的路径预测集；2）引入残差保形值网络（RCVNet），通过PUCT引导探索来学习更具区分性的路径非一致性分数。

Result: 在公开数据集上，CPR方法相较于保形预测基线，提升了34%的经验覆盖率，并使预测集平均大小减少40%。

Abstract: Knowledge Graph Question Answering (KGQA) has shown promise for grounded and interpretable reasoning, yet existing approaches often fail to provide reliable coverage guarantees over retrieved answers. While Conformal Prediction (CP) offers a principled framework for producing prediction sets with statistical guarantees, prior methods suffer from critical limitations in both calibration validity and score discriminability, resulting in violated coverage guarantees and excessively large prediction sets. To address these pitfalls, we propose Conformal Path Reasoning (CPR), a trustworthy KGQA framework with two key innovations. First, we perform query-level conformal calibration over path-level scores, preserving the exchangeability while generating path prediction sets. Second, we introduce the Residual Conformal Value Network (RCVNet), a lightweight module trained via PUCT-guided exploration to learn discriminative path-level nonconformity scores. Experiments on benchmarks show that CPR significantly improves the Empirical Coverage Rate by 34% while reducing average prediction set size by 40% compared to conformal baselines. These results validate the efficacy of CPR in satisfying coverage guarantees with substantially more compact answer sets.

### [244] [LLMs Improving LLMs: Agentic Discovery for Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08083)
*Tong Zheng,Haolin Liu,Chengsong Huang,Huiwen Bao,Sheng Zhang,Rui Liu,Runpeng Dai,Ruibo Chen,Chenxi Liu,Tianyi Xiong,Xidong Wu,Hongming Zhang,Heng Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种环境驱动的自动测试时缩放（AutoTTS）框架，通过在自动构建的环境中搜索推理策略，有效提升大语言模型在推理阶段的表现，并优于手工设计的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时缩放（TTS）方法大多依赖于手工设计的启发式规则，覆盖面有限且探索空间不足，因此需要一种可以自动发现更优TTS策略的新方法。

Method: 作者提出AutoTTS框架，核心是通过环境建设，使TTS策略的发现过程自动化。具体做法包括：1）将宽度—深度TTS问题表述为控制器合成任务，利用预收集的推理轨迹和探针信号，控制器可决定何时分支、继续、探测、修剪或停止。2）采用beta参数化方法简化搜索空间，3）引入细粒度执行反馈，帮助诊断策略失败的原因，从而提升搜索效率。

Result: 在数学推理基准上，所发现的AutoTTS策略在准确率与计算成本权衡方面，超过了强有力的手工基线方法。AutoTTS发现的策略在未见过的数据与不同模型规模上也表现出了良好泛化性。整个策略发现过程仅耗费$39.9和160分钟。

Conclusion: AutoTTS成功实现了TTS策略的自动发现，解决了手工设计探索空间有限的问题，提升了大模型测试阶段的推理能力。其方法泛化性强，计算开销低，有望被广泛应用于各类推理任务。

Abstract: Test-time scaling (TTS) has become an effective approach for improving large language model performance by allocating additional computation during inference. However, existing TTS strategies are largely hand-crafted: researchers manually design reasoning patterns and tune heuristics by intuition, leaving much of the computation-allocation space unexplored. We propose an environment-driven framework, AutoTTS, that changes what researchers design: from individual TTS heuristics to environments where TTS strategies can be discovered automatically. The key to AutoTTS lies in environment construction: the discovery environment must make the control space tractable and provide cheap, frequent feedback for TTS search. As a concrete instantiation, we formulate width--depth TTS as controller synthesis over pre-collected reasoning trajectories and probe signals, where controllers decide when to branch, continue, probe, prune, or stop and can be evaluated cheaply without repeated LLM calls. We further introduce beta parameterization to make the search tractable and fine-grained execution trace feedback to improve discovery efficiency by helping the agent diagnose why a TTS program fails. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that the discovered strategies improve the overall accuracy--cost tradeoff over strong manually designed baselines. The discovered strategies generalize to held-out benchmarks and model scales, while the entire discovery costs only $39.9 and 160 minutes. Our data, and code will be open-source at https://github.com/zhengkid/AutoTTS.

</details>

### [245] [Modular Lie Algebraic PDE Control of Multibody Flexible Manipulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06709)
*Sadeq Yaqubi,Jouni Mattila*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对柔性机械臂的基于PDE和螺旋理论的控制方法，能实现高精度、全局指数收敛的末端控制及参数自适应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 柔性多体机器人因轻量化和安全需要被广泛应用，但其柔性和多体耦合效应导致建模和控制极为复杂，现有方法常难以适应复杂变形和参数不确定性的情况。该工作旨在提出一个能泛化、可扩展、并且稳定性有理论保证的新型控制框架。

Method: 1) 用基于螺旋理论的李代数模型(se(3))统一表达运动、变形和力；2) 采用基于应变的PDE动态替代普通动力学方程，消去弹性加速度——即用微分方程描述连续柔性体的动力学；3) 通过任务空间逆解补偿柔性末端偏差，生成实时修正的姿态轨迹；4) 每个子系统（链节）配Lyapunov函数实现指数收敛控制，并支持参数在线自适应估计；5) 设计级联Lyapunov函数，利用动力学和相互作用消元，理论证明跟踪误差收敛和弹性变形有界。

Result: 动力学模型实现了弹性加速度的消元与系统稳定性全局指数收敛保证；提出的控制器不仅可以实时消除末端形变量，还可在线自适应估计系统参数；理论证明相互作用完全消元，且所有收敛结果均可扩展至任意长度串联机械臂。数值仿真验证了物理一致性和模型准确性。

Conclusion: 该PDE-螺旋理论控制框架适用于多体柔性机器人系统，控制方法具有模块化、可扩展及严格稳定性保证，能够实时补偿端部柔性偏差，对于实际柔性机器人结构的精确控制和工程部署具有重要意义。

Abstract: This paper addresses PDE-based control for flexible multibody robotic systems, presenting a subsystem-based framework for serial manipulators with arbitrary links in 3D space. The approach uses a screw-theoretic Lie-algebraic model where motion, deformation, and forces are expressed as body-fixed twists and wrenches in se(3). By substituting a strain-based deformation PDE into the dynamics, distributed elastic acceleration is eliminated, yielding a model governed by twist acceleration and the deformation field. Subsystem twist trajectories are generated from task-space endpoints via deflection-compensating inverse kinematics, providing real-time correction for tip deformation. A nominal controller for each link ensures exponential decay of twist errors via a Lyapunov function nu_i. An adaptive modification replaces physical parameters with online estimates, establishing exponential convergence of both twist and parameter errors. Summing over all links, composite Lyapunov functions V = sum(nu_i) and V^a = sum(nu_i^a) yield time derivatives where inter-link interaction power terms telescope to zero. This cancellation is ensured by Newton's third law and the frame invariance of the power pairing on se(3) x se*(3), establishing global exponential convergence of tracking errors. Bounded elastic deformation is guaranteed by an Euler-Bernoulli energy argument. The screw-theoretic structure renders interaction cancellation exact, making the stability certificate modular and scalable to chains of arbitrary length. Numerical simulations demonstrate the scheme's physical consistency.

</details>


### [246] [An Aerial Manipulator for Perception-Driven Flower Targeting Toward Contactless Pollination in Vertical Farming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06759)
*Chenzhe Jin,Zhuohang Wu,Yifan Cai,Xiangqi Li,Jan Ming Kevin Tan,Narsimlu Kemsaram,Valerio Modugno*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套空中机器人平台，用于精准定位与接近花朵，为未来室内农业授粉提供基础。该平台集成了图像感知、MPPI控制与2自由度机械臂，实现了高精度操作，并在仿真与实验证明了其实用性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自然传粉昆虫数量锐减，特别是在垂直农业等室内环境下，传统依赖昆虫的授粉方式难以实现。这对作物生产带来严重挑战，因此迫切需要开发能够替代自然授粉的机器人系统。

Result: 实验和仿真显示：平台能够实现飞行器稳定飞行、可靠花朵定位及厘米级末端定位精度。控制器具备良好的轨迹收敛性和目标对准能力，系统在受限空域内亦能完成花朵定位与末端对准，展现出高度的实用性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: The decline of natural pollinators has created a major challenge for crop production in controlled indoor agriculture, particularly in vertical farming environments where natural insect pollination is absent. This motivates the development of robotic systems capable of performing precise flower targeting tasks while minimizing physical interference with delicate floral structures. This paper presents an aerial manipulator platform for perception driven flower detection, localization, and approach in vertical farming environments. The proposed system integrates onboard RGBD based perception, model predictive path integral (MPPI) based unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) control on a PX4 platform, and a lightweight 2DoF manipulator for precise end effector positioning. The platform is evaluated in both MuJoCo simulation and UAV lab experiments using a flower targeting testbed. The experimental results demonstrate stable UAV flight, reliable flower localization, and centimeter level end effector positioning accuracy. In simulation, the proposed controller achieves consistent trajectory convergence and accurate target alignment. In the real world UAV lab environment, the integrated perception control manipulation framework enables stable flower targeted positioning and end effector alignment under constrained aerial operation. These results validate the proposed aerial manipulator as a robust robotic carrier and positioning framework for future contactless pollination systems. While the current study focuses on perception guided targeting and positioning, the developed platform provides a practical foundation for integrating advanced contactless end effectors, including acoustic based pollen manipulation modules, in future work.

### [250] [Intention assimilation control for accurate tracking with variable impedance in teleoperation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07037)
*Atsushi Takagi,Yanan Li,Hiroaki Gomi,Etienne Burdet*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统远程操作机器人采用弹簧式力控制，使得机器人的跟踪精度和操作安全性存在权衡：高刚度提升精度但增加安全隐患，低刚度则精度下降。需要新的控制策略来兼顾安全与性能。

Method: 提出IAC控制策略，不再传递领导者当前位置，而是估算其目标位置并传递给跟随者。该方法允许实时变更机器人的阻抗，既可反映用户意图，又可自动调整以满足任务需求。在两个7自由度机械臂上进行了实验，包括自由跟踪、气球交互、插销和桌面抛光。

Result: 实验结果显示IAC方法在不同阻抗下均能实现高跟踪精度。与远程阻抗控制（TIC）相比，IAC提升了精度、任务完成率并减少了完成所需时间。

Conclusion: IAC方法可在单向和双向远程操作中，精确重现用户运动并灵活调节机械臂阻抗，实现更高水平的操作控制和平衡安全性。

Abstract: Robot systems for teleoperation commonly use a spring-like force pulling the follower robot towards the leader's position to track their movements. With this control strategy, the tracking accuracy deteriorates when the follower' stiffness is low, but high stiffness poses a danger to objects or people in the follower robot's environment. To address this trade-off between tracking accuracy and safety, we propose an alternative intention assimilation control (IAC) strategy where the robot's tracking accuracy can be ensured without high stiffness. Different from traditional approaches, which transmit the leader's current position to the follower, this new controller estimates the leader's target position and transmits it to the follower. With this strategy, the follower impedance can be changed on-the-fly to continuously reflect the user's desired impedance or modulated automatically to fulfill the task requirements. Our controller was validated on two 7 degree-of-freedom manipulators, yielding high tracking accuracy with varying impedance. Four experiments were conducted to compare {teleoperation} with IAC to tele-impedance control (TIC) during free tracking, interaction with a balloon, during peg insertion, and table polishing with force feedback. The results show that IAC increases tracking accuracy, improves task completion rate and reduces completion time. IAC enables the robot to accurately replicate the user's movement while giving them freedom to modulate the impedance according to their intention, providing an unprecedented level of control of the follower's position and its impedance during unilateral and bilateral teleoperation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Dr-BA直接利用多个雷达扫描的2D强度图全量信息，通过可分离优化，将姿态估计和地图重建解耦，既能做联合建图，又能进行纯雷达定位。该方法不抽取稀疏点，而是用密集图像进行端到端优化。

Abstract: This paper introduces Dr-BA, a first-of-its-kind radar bundle adjustment (BA) framework that operates directly on 2D spinning radar intensity images. Unlike camera or lidar sensors, radar is largely unaffected by precipitation, making it a critical modality for autonomous systems that require all-weather robustness. Existing state estimation approaches using spinning radar typically extract sparse point clouds from range-azimuth-intensity measurements and apply point cloud alignment techniques to estimate vehicle motion, scene structure, or to localize within an existing map. In contrast, Dr-BA uses the full radar returns from multiple scans to jointly estimate dense maps and sensor poses. By formulating the problem as a separable optimization, we derive an efficient and general solution that decouples pose estimation from mapping. In addition to solving the BA problem, this formulation naturally extends to direct radar-only localization (DRL) within a previously built map. Dr-BA achieves state-of-the-art radar-based BA and cross-session localization performance, demonstrated on more than 200 km of on-road data across five distinct routes. Our implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/utiasASRL/dr_ba.

### [252] [PISTO: Proximal Inference for Stochastic Trajectory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07215)
*Hongzhe Yu,Zinuo Chang,Yongxin Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了PISTO算法，通过KL正则化增强STOMP优势，实现了更高效、更稳定的无导数轨迹优化，且在多项基准任务中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: STOMP等随机轨迹优化方法虽然可以处理不可微分的代价函数，但算法稳定性和收敛性仍有限。作者希望改善优化过程的稳定性和性能，并赋予其更坚实的理论基础。

Method: 作者首先揭示STOMP实际是在最小化Boltzmann轨迹分布的KL散度，表现出变分推断结构。基于此，提出PISTO算法：在优化目标中增加连续高斯分布提案间的KL正则化，形成近端（trust-region）结构，并通过重要性加权蒙特卡洛采样计算期望，从而实现一个无需导数、稳定高效的新算法。

Result: 在机器人臂运动规划基准测试中，PISTO成功率达89%，优于CHOMP（63%）和STOMP（68%），且以更快的速度生成更短、更平滑的路径。在MuJoCo接触任务中，PISTO在奖励上持续超越CEM和MPPI。

Conclusion: PISTO不仅理论上优雅地统一了轨迹优化中的变分推断结构，也在广泛基准任务上实证显示其性能和泛化能力，展现了明显优于现有无导数轨迹优化方法的优势。

Abstract: Stochastic trajectory optimization methods like STOMP enable planning with non-differentiable costs, offering substantial flexibility over gradient-based approaches. We show that STOMP implicitly minimizes the KL divergence from a Boltzmann trajectory distribution, revealing an elegant Variational Inference (VI) structure underlying its updates. Building on this insight, we propose the \textit{Proximal Inference for Stochastic Trajectory Optimization} (PISTO) algorithm that stabilizes the updates by augmenting the objective with a KL regularization between successive Gaussian proposals. This proximal formulation admits a trust-region interpretation and yields closed-form mean updates computable as expectations under a surrogate distribution. We estimate these expectations via importance-weighted Monte Carlo sampling, producing a simple, derivative-free algorithm that inherits STOMP's ability to handle non-differentiable and discontinuous costs without modification. On robot arm motion planning benchmarks, PISTO achieves an 89\% success rate -- outperforming CHOMP (63\%) and STOMP (68\%) -- while producing shorter, smoother paths at twice the speed of competing stochastic methods. We further validate PISTO on contact-rich MuJoCo locomotion and manipulation tasks, where it consistently outperforms both CEM and MPPI baselines in reward.

</details>

This paper presents a lightweight autonomous exploration system that leverages omnidirectional vision and sparse topological map guidance. Specifically, we utilize a multi-fisheye camera setup to achieve omnidirectional Field of View (FoV) and perform depth estimation. To address the limited depth estimation accuracy, frontiers are represented as potential unexplored regions characterized by topological nodes instead of explicit boundaries, enabling efficient identification of frontier regions without maintaining occupancy grids or global point clouds. Unlike classic dense representations, our approach abstracts the environment using a sparse topological map composed of key nodes and their descriptors, reducing memory consumption and computational demands. Global path planning is performed directly on the sparse graph. The proposed method is validated in both simulation and on a palm-sized vision-based UAV with an 11 cm wheelbase and a 400 g weight in real-world experiments, demonstrating that our method can achieve efficient exploration with extremely low computational consumption.

### [254] [Variable Aerodynamic Damping via Co-Contraction: A Dynamic Isomorphism with Variable Stiffness Actuators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07292)
*Antonio Franchi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出并证明了在冗余双转子执行器中，通过气动“共收缩”操作能够调节系统的被动阻尼，同时保持总推力不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着灵巧机器人和无人机发展，对动力学调谐（尤其被动阻尼和刚度）的需求越来越高。传统方法常需能耗提升或硬件复杂化，作者试图探索气动方式下能否如生物肌肉共激活（共收缩）实现被动参数调节，从而提升多旋翼系统的动态表现。

Method: 论文定义了一个增量阻尼系数来量化该调控效应，并在常力条件下分析其变化趋势，利用Blade Element Theory推导出气动模型，证明该阻尼可通过共收缩单调调节。还进一步把该机制形式化为‘可变气动阻尼执行器’（VADA），并建立与可变刚度致动（VSA）的动力学同构关系。

Result: 数学证明该机制成立，并通过一阶原理推导的模型验证了所需气动特性，还揭示了常力“纤维密度”对多旋翼系统的动态响应有效提升。

Conclusion: 气动共收缩为多旋翼等冗余驱动系统提供了一条无需额外能耗即可灵活调节被动阻尼的全新技术途径，也为动力学参数的生物启发式控制奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We prove that aerodynamic co-contraction in a redundant dual-rotor actuator can tune a passive, trim-defined aero-mechanical damping while keeping the commanded net force constant. In particular, we define an incremental damping coefficient as the local sensitivity of net thrust to air-relative velocity at a trim and prove that it increases monotonically along constant-force fibers under a mild aerodynamic hardening condition. We then validate the required damping and hardening properties from a first-principles Blade Element Theory derivation, which yields a minimal thrust model affine in inflow and explicitly reveals the speed--inflow coupling driving the effect. The resulting mechanism is formalized as a Variable Aerodynamic Damping Actuator (VADA) and shown to be dynamically isomorphic to stiffness modulation in antagonistic variable-stiffness actuation (VSA), similar to the co-contraction of tendons by muscle co-activation. The same fiber-density principle also enhances the active aerodynamic promptness measure of redundant multirotors. Finally, an impedance-form representation clarifies the roles of common-mode and differential-mode actuation in the control of passive impedance and the equilibrium velocity of the VADA system.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前生物实验室自动化面临多项挑战，如实验协议结构不明确、透明/反光实验器具影响感知、多步骤操作需持续状态感知，以及现有自动化系统成本高、流程固定和设备专有等问题。亟需一种经济高效、通用性强且抗干扰的自动化解决方案。

Method: 论文提出了BioProVLA-Agent系统，包括：1）协议解析智能体——利用LLM将实验协议转译为可验证的子任务；2）视觉-语言-检索智能体——根据现场感知判断任务准备/完成状态；3）VLA体态执行智能体——以轻量策略执行经过验证的子任务。结合在线视觉增强（AugSmolVLA）方法提升对各种视觉干扰（如透明器具、反射、光照变化等）的鲁棒性。

Result: 系统在15个基础任务、6个复合流程和3个双手操作任务的分层基准测试中评估，包括管道装载、分类、废弃、瓶盖旋拧和液体倾倒等。实验证明，AugSmolVLA显著提升了BioProVLA-Agent在常规和高曝光等不同视觉条件下的操作稳定性，优于对比方法（ACT、X-VLA、SmolVLA），尤其在精确放置、透明物体操作、复杂流程和视觉退化场景下表现突出。

Conclusion: BioProVLA-Agent为生物实验操作自动化提供了一条易获得、以协议为核心、具备视觉状态验证能力的现实途径，有望大幅提升生物实验室的操作自动化和效率。

Abstract: Biological laboratory automation can reduce repetitive manual work and improve reproducibility, but reliable embodied execution in wet-lab environments remains challenging. Protocols are often unstructured, labware is frequently transparent or reflective, and multi-step procedures require state-aware execution beyond one-shot instruction following. Existing robotic systems often rely on costly hardware, fixed workflows, dedicated instruments, or robotics-oriented interfaces. Here, we introduce BioProVLA-Agent, an affordable, protocol-driven, vision-enhanced embodied multi-agent system enabled by Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models for biological manipulation. The system uses protocols as the task interface and integrates protocol parsing, visual state verification, and embodied execution in a closed-loop workflow. A Tailored LLM Protocol Agent converts protocols into verifiable subtasks; a VLM-RAG Verification Agent assesses readiness and completion using observations, robot states, retrieved knowledge, and success/failure examples; and a VLA Embodied Agent executes verified subtasks through a lightweight policy. To improve robustness under wet-lab visual perturbations, we develop AugSmolVLA, an online augmentation strategy targeting transparent labware, reflections, illumination shifts, and overexposure. We evaluate the system on a hierarchical benchmark covering 15 atomic tasks, 6 composite workflows, and 3 bimanual tasks, including tube loading, sorting, waste disposal, cap twisting, and liquid pouring. Across normal and high-exposure settings, AugSmolVLA improves execution stability over ACT, X-VLA, and the original SmolVLA, especially for precise placement, transparent-object manipulation, composite workflows, and visually degraded scenes. These results suggest a practical route toward accessible, protocol-centered, and verification-capable embodied AI for biological manipulation.

### [256] [AT-VLA: Adaptive Tactile Injection for Enhanced Feedback Reaction in Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07308)
*Xiaoqi Li,Muhe Cai,Jiadong Xu,Juan Zhu,Hongwei Fan,Yan Shen,Guangrui Ren,Hao Dong*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了自适应触觉视觉-语言-动作（AT-VLA）模型，通过引入创新的触觉注入机制和双流感知处理，提升了机器人在复杂物理交互任务中的实时性能和准确性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视-言-动（VLA）模型在需要精细物理互动的任务中表现受限，主要是由于对触觉信号的利用不足和推理速度慢，影响了机器人操作的灵活性和效率。

Method: 作者提出了AT-VLA框架，包含两大创新：1）自适应触觉注入机制，根据当前任务动态决定触觉信号的注入时机与位置，仅在对动作生成有明显贡献时加入，减少对预训练表征的干扰；2）触觉反应双流机制，将感知处理分为慢速的视觉-语言流（处理低频感知推理）和快速的触觉控制流（理解高频物理交互），实现0.04秒内的实时闭环响应。

Result: 在真实环境下的多项接触丰富操作任务中，AT-VLA表现优异，实验结果验证了其能够高效、准确地融合触觉反馈，提升机器人完成复杂任务的能力。

Conclusion: AT-VLA成功突破了传统VLA模型的触觉整合瓶颈和慢速响应局限，实现了高效、实时的触觉-视觉-语言动作协同，为机器人复杂操作能力提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have significantly advanced the capabilities of robotic agents in executing diverse tasks; however, they still face challenges in contact-rich manipulation scenarios that require precise physical interactions. To address this limitation, recent studies have attempted to incorporate tactile signals during downstream tasks, enabling pretrained VLAs to interpret tactile feedback. Nevertheless, introducing new modalities during finetuning, which are rarely present in the pretrain stage, may disrupt the pretrained capabilities of VLAs. In addition, the inherently slow inference speed of VLAs hampers real-time responsiveness and limits the effective utilization of tactile feedback for action adjustment. To overcome these challenges, we propose Adaptive Tactile Vision-Language-Action (AT-VLA), which introduces a novel Adaptive Tactile Injection mechanism. This mechanism dynamically determines the appropriate timing and locations for tactile injection, incorporating only when it significantly contributes to action generation, thereby minimizing interference with pretrained representations. Furthermore, to enable rapid and accurate tactile responses, we propose a Tactile Reaction Dual-Stream mechanism, which decouples sensory processing into a slow visual-language stream for low-frequency perceptual reasoning and a fast tactile control stream for high-frequency physical interaction understanding, achieving real-time close-loop responses within 0.04 s. Real-world experiments thoroughly validate the effectiveness of AT-VLA in contact-rich manipulation tasks. The project page is available at: https://sites.google.com/view/at-vla.

### [257] [CSR: Infinite-Horizon Real-Time Policies with Massive Cached State Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07325)
*Robin Karlsson,Go Suzui*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新框架（CSR和ASR），极大降低大模型在机器人连续推理中的响应延迟，实现了大幅加速和效果提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人等场景中，需要大语言模型持续处理复杂且长时序的状态历史，但现有做法如RAG或滑动窗口存在上下文丢失或计算量过大，导致响应延迟过高，难以实时应用。

Method: 理论上分析并证明了降低延迟的最优任务结构需要前缀稳定性、增量可扩展性和异步状态对齐。基于此，提出了Cached State Representation（CSR）及Asynchronous State Reconciliation（ASR）两个具体算法，实现KV-cache重用和异步状态管理，提升处理效率。

Result: 实验证明，CSR在实际机器人和235B参数大模型上将延迟从14.67秒降低到0.56秒（提升26倍），同时提升回忆准确率至SOTA水平，ASR可在长时间连续运行下持续稳定延迟表现。

Conclusion: 该工作为大模型实时应用于机器人和高频交互场景提供了可行的系统方法，显著突破时间延迟与上下文保留的矛盾。

Abstract: Deploying massive large language models (LLMs) as continuous cognitive engines for robotics is bottlenecked by the time-to-first-token (TTFT) latency required to process extensive state histories. Existing solutions like RAG or sliding windows compromise global context or incur prohibitive re-computation costs. We formalize the optimal task structure for minimizing latency and theoretically prove that prefix stability, incremental extensibility, and asynchronous state reconciliation are necessary conditions for real-time performance. Building on these proofs, we introduce the Cached State Representation (CSR) framework as the practical instantiation of these properties, ensuring optimal KV-cache reuse. To sustain these properties over infinite horizons, we further propose an Asynchronous State Reconciliation (ASR) algorithm that offloads state memory eviction to a parallel computational resource to eliminate latency spikes. On a physical robot wirelessly connected to an on-premise GPU server, CSR achieves a 26-fold latency reduction (14.67s to 0.56s) for 120K token contexts with a 235B parameter model compared to a standard baseline. On an embodied AI benchmark, we achieve SOTA recall (0.836 vs. 0.459) while maintaining RAG-level latency. ASR is validated to sustain bounded, spike-free TTFT over 10 eviction cycles in continuous real-world operation. Together, CSR and ASR enable massive LLMs to function as continuously operating, high-frequency (> 2 Hz) embodied policies.

Conclusion: 毫米波雷达在恶劣天气下具备优越的稳定性，通过有效的编码和正则化方法，可使冻结的视觉-语言模型适配雷达数据。相关结构与策略的权衡分析有助于未来雷达-视觉语言多模态管线的设计。

Abstract: Cameras and LiDAR degrade in rain, fog, and snow, while millimeter-wave radar remains largely unaffected. We align a radar encoder to frozen SigLIP vision
  embeddings and decode structured scene captions through a frozen vision-language model (VLM) with approximately 7M trainable parameters. On K-RADAR with
  held-out fog, light snow, and heavy snow sequences, all radar configurations outperform a camera baseline that collapses to over 90% hallucination. We
  identify a token-norm mismatch as the dominant failure mode when bridging radar to a frozen VLM and show that projector-output LayerNorm resolves it.
  Analysis of encoder complexity, caption format, and pooling strategy reveals tradeoffs that inform future radar-VLM pipeline design.

### [259] [MORPH-U: Multi-Objective Resilient Motion Planning for V2X-Enabled Autonomous Driving in High-Uncertainty Environments via Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07370)
*Shih-Yu Lai*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管V2X能扩展自动驾驶车辆的感知范围，但由于信息不可靠（延迟、丢包、伪造等），且地图实时变化，现有方法难以安全高效地实时规划与控制。因此需要一种能兼容V2X不确定信息且具备安全防护的控制栈。

Method: 提出MORPH-U系统，利用LiDAR、雷达、摄像头和V2X信息融合成本地动态地图（LDM），结合事件触发的Hybrid-A*路线重规划。采用多目标优化分析规划与控制间关于精度、安全、响应和舒适的权衡，通过Pareto前沿调参实现平衡。为防止恶意虚假信息触发不安全重规划，设计轻量级类拜占庭容错门控机制，将一致性投票和车载传感器否决结合。

Result: 仿真实验表明，V2X参与的本地动态地图显著提升了安全性；Pareto调参有效实现了性能的多目标权衡；新设计的门控机制能抵御100%虚假信息攻击，避免误规划。

Conclusion: MORPH-U融合多源信息并具备针对V2X不确定性的安全防护机制，为自动驾驶在真实不可靠外部环境下的安全规划与控制提供了有效方案。

Abstract: V2X can warn an autonomous vehicle about hazards beyond line-of-sight, but it also brings uncertainty: messages may be delayed, dropped, or even forged. Meanwhile, map knowledge may change during a trip, forcing the vehicle to replan under tight real-time budgets. This paper studies how to make motion planning and low-level control robust to such uncertain, event-driven updates. We present MORPH-U, a CARLA-based closed-loop stack that fuses LiDAR/radar/camera with V2X (CAM/DENM) into a Local Dynamic Map (LDM) and triggers Hybrid-A* replanning when validated hazards or map changes affect the planned route. We expose the planning/control trade-offs via a multi-objective formulation over tracking error, safety margin (minimum TTC), responsiveness, and smoothness, and select operating points using Pareto-frontier analysis. To avoid unsafe replanning from faulty V2X triggers, MORPH-U adds a lightweight Byzantine-inspired acceptance gate that combines a quorum rule with an on-board sensor veto. Experiments in dynamic CARLA scenarios show that V2X-augmented LDM improves downstream safety, Pareto tuning provides controllable accuracy-comfort trade-offs, and the gate prevents replanning under saturated false-DENM injection ($p_{\text{attack}}=1.0$).
